diff -ruN linux-5.9.1/kernel/sys.c mylinux-5.9.1/kernel/sys.c
--- linux-5.9.1/kernel/sys.c	2020-10-17 12:01:22.000000000 +0530
+++ mylinux-5.9.1/kernel/sys.c	2020-11-22 11:24:20.135375728 +0530

 		return -EFAULT;

 }
+
+SYSCALL_DEFINE2(rt_nice, long, pid, long, tim)
+{
+	struct task_struct *task;
+	
+	if(pid > 32768 || pid <= 0)
+	{
+		printk("Invalid pid value!!\n");
+		return -EINVAL;
+	}
+	
+	if(tim < 0)
+	{
+		printk("Invalid soft time value!!\n");
+		return -EINVAL;
+	}
+	
+	task = find_task_by_vpid((pid_t)pid);
+
+	if(!task){
+		printk("No such process found!!\n");
+		return -ESRCH;
+	}
+	
+	printk("Changed soft_runtime value:  %s\n", task->comm);
+	task->se.soft_runtime = tim;
+	
+	printk("Done!");
+	
+	printk("\n\n");
+	
+	return 0;
+}

+/* x86 opcode map generated from x86-opcode-map.txt */
+/* Do not change this code. */
+
+/* Table: one byte opcode */
+const insn_attr_t inat_primary_table[INAT_OPCODE_TABLE_SIZE] = {
+	[0x00] = INAT_MODRM,
+	[0x01] = INAT_MODRM,
+	[0x02] = INAT_MODRM,
+	[0x03] = INAT_MODRM,
